# HKMU Public Programme Course Collection Skill

## Scope and Accuracy Notes

- University: Hong Kong Metropolitan University (HKMU).
- Source type: official publicly accessible HKMU Programme Requirements PDFs.
- Coverage target: undergraduate and sub-degree programme requirements listed on HKMU public pages for both the 5-credit System and 3-credit-unit System.
- Important limitation: HKMU's public Course Search page says class schedules and pre-requisites are provided through MyHKMU > Programme > Classes & Enrolment > Enrolment - UG.
- When a Programme Requirements PDF does not state an actual term/semester, courses are grouped under the official table heading and marked `Not specified in public PDF` for semester.

## Official Source Pages

- Programme Requirements (5-credit System): https://www.hkmu.edu.hk/undergraduate-students/course-enrolment/programme-requirements/
- Programme Requirements (3-credit-unit System): https://www.hkmu.edu.hk/undergraduate-students/course-enrolment/programme-requirements-3cru/
- Course Search note: https://www.hkmu.edu.hk/undergraduate-students/course-enrolment/course-search/

## Collection Summary

- Programme requirement PDFs discovered: 139
- Programme requirement PDFs parsed: 139
- Programme-course rows extracted: 4768

|   |   |   +-- Global Immersion Programme (Undergraduate Year 4) 1. With effect from the 2022 Spring Term, MGT B399F has been replaced by MGT B398F. If students have successfully completed MGT B399F, they are deemed to have satisfied the requirements of MGT B398F. 2. Students who have completed BUS B086F would be deemed to have completed the requirements for BUS B083F, and vice versa. Honours Classification For the calculation of honours classification of the Bachelor of Business Administration with Honours in Business Intelligence and Analytics programme, the best 80 credits in Higher or Middle Level courses will be counted. Among the 80 credits, 40 credits shall be from Group (a) courses and another 40 credits from Group (b) courses. Group (a) courses shall consist of the best 40 credits from Higher Level courses listed in Tables 4, 5, 6 and 7. Group (b) courses shall consist of the best 40 credits from courses at Higher or Middle Level listed in Tables 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6 and 7 , where such credits are not taken into account in Group (a) courses. Further, Group (a) courses shall be weighted the same as Group (b) courses. For students admitted before the 2018/19 academic year A student admitted to the programme through Year 1 Entry needs to complete a total of 160 credits and of which no more than 40 credits should be taken at Foundation Level. A student is required to complete: 1. 70 credits of core courses in Tables 9, 10 and 11; 2. 15 credits of prescribed courses in Table 12; 3. 50 credits of prescribed concentration courses in Table 13; 4. 5 credits of a business elective course from Table 14; and 5. 20 credits of purpose-designed General Education courses#. # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE). A student admitted to the programme through Year 2 Entry needs to complete a total of 120 credits and of which no more than 20 credits should be taken at Foundation Level. A student is required to complete: 1. 35 credits of core courses in Tables 9 and 10; 2. 5 credits of a core course in Table 11; 3. 15 credits of prescribed courses in Table 12; 4. 50 credits of prescribed concentration courses in Table 13; 5. 5 credits of a business elective course from Table 14; and 6. 10 credits of purpose-designed General Education courses#. # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE). Honours Classification For the calculation of honours classification of the Bachelor of Business Administration with Honours in Global Business and Marketing programme, the best 80 credits in Higher or Middle Level courses will be counted. Among the 80 credits, 40 credits shall be from Group (a) courses and another 40 credits from Group (b) courses. Group (a) courses shall consist of the best 40 credits from Higher Level courses listed in Tables 5, 6, 7 and 8. Group (b) courses shall consist of the best 40 credits from courses at Higher or Middle Level listed in the Tables 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7 and 8, where such credits are not taken into account in Group (a) courses. Further, Group (a) courses shall be weighted the same as Group (b) courses. For students admitted before the 2018/19 academic year A student admitted to the programme through Year 1 Entry needs to complete a total of 160 A student is required to complete: 1. 70 credits of core courses from Tables 10, 11 and 12; 2. 15 credits of prescribed courses in Table 13; 3. 50 credits of prescribed concentration courses in Table 14; 4. 5 credits of a business elective course from Table 15; and 5. 20 credits of purpose-designed General Education courses#. # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE). A student admitted to the programme through Year 2 Entry needs to complete a total of 120 A student is required to complete: 1. 35 credits of core courses from Tables 10 and 11; 2. 5 credits of a core course in Table 12; 3. 15 credits of prescribed courses in Table 13; 4. 50 credits of prescribed concentration courses in Table 14; 5. 5 credits of a business elective course from Table 15; and 6. 10 credits of purpose-designed General Education courses#. # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE). A student admitted to the programme through Year 3 Entry needs to complete a total of [代码: MKT B461F] [学分: 80]

Honours Classification For the calculation of honours classification for the Bachelor of Business Administration with Honours in Professional Accounting programme, the best 80 credits in Higher or Middle Level courses will be counted. Among the 80 credits, 40 credits shall be f rom Group (a) courses and another 40 credits from Group (b) courses. Group (a) shall consist of the best 40 credits from the Higher Level courses listed in Tables 5, 6, [代码: MGT B397F] [学分: 7]
|   |   |
|   |   +-- Not specified in public PDF | Global Immersion Programmes/
|   |   |   +-- IB B397F 4. Students who have completed BUS B086F would be deemed to have completed the requirements for BUS B083F , and vice versa. Honours Classification For the calculation of honours classification for the Bachelor of Business Administration with Honours in Professional Accounting programme, the best 80 credits in Higher or Middle Level courses will be counted. Among the 80 credits, 40 credits shall be from Group (a) courses and another 40 credits from Group (b) courses. Group (a) shall consist of the best 40 credits from the Higher Level courses listed in Tables 14, 15, 16 and 17. Group (b) shall consist of the best 40 credits from courses at Higher or Middle Level listed in the Tables 10, 11, 12, 13, 14, 15, 16 and 17, where such credits are not taken into account in Group (a). Further, Group (a) courses shall be weighted the same as Group (b) courses. For students admitted before the 2018/19 academic year A student admitted to the programme through Year 1 Entry is required to complete a total of 160 1. 70 credits of core courses in Tables 19, 20 and 21; 2. 15 credits of prescribed courses in Table 22; 3. 45 credits of prescribed concentration courses in Table 23; 4. 10 credits of business elective courses in Table 24; and 5. 20 credits of purpose-designed General Education courses#. # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE). A student admitted to the programme through Year 2 Entry is required to complete a total of 120 1. 35 credits of core courses from Tables 19 and 20, of which 5 credits must be from LAW B262F; 2. 5 credits of a core course in Table 21; 3. 15 credits of prescribed courses in Table 22; 4. 45 credits of prescribed concentration courses in Table 23; 5. 10 credits of business elective courses from Table 24; and 6. 10 credits of purpose-designed General Education courses# # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE). A student admitted to the programme through Year 3 Entry is required to complete a total of [代码: MGT B397F] [学分: 85]

|   |   |   +-- (5 credits) IB B392F (5 credits) 7. With effect from the 2021 Autumn term, BUS B104F , COMR B208F , LAW B262F and SPM B214F have been replaced by BUS B220F . If students have successfully completed BUS B104F , COMR B208F , LAW B262F and SPM B214F , they are deemed to have satisfied the requirements of BUS B220F . 8. Effective from 2022 Spring Term, students are required to take MGT B398F instead of MGT B399F . Students should note that MGT B398F CANNOT be used to claim exemption from any professional accounting/corporate governance examination papers. School’ s prior approval is required if students would like to enroll to MGT B399F instead of MGT B398F to fulfill the programme requirement. Students who have previously completed MGT B399F are deemed to have completed the requirements for MGT B398F . Period of Study The Bachelor of International Hospitality and Attractions Management with Honours (Year 3 entry) provides options for students to study on a full-time or part-time basis. The normative period of study is listed below: Full-time study : 2 years Part-time study : 3.5 years Honours Classification For the calculation of honours classification of the Bachelor of International Hospitality and Attractions Management with Honours , the best 80 credits in Higher or Middle Level courses will be counted. Among the 80 credits, 40 credits shall be from Group (a) courses and another [代码: MKT B392F] [学分: 40]

School’ s prior approval is required if students would like to enroll to MGT B399F instead of MGT B398F to fulfill the programme requirement. Students who have previously completed MGT B399F are deemed to have completed the requirements for MGT B398F . Period of Study The Bachelor of International Hospitality and Attractions Management with Honours (Year 3 entry) provides options for students to study on a full -time or part-time basis. The normative period of study is listed below: Full-time study : 2 years Part-time study : 3.5 years Honours Classification For the calcul ation of honours classification of the Bachelor of International Hospitality and Attractions Management with Honours , the best 80 credits in Higher or Middle Level courses will be counted. |   |   |   +-- CCA A351CF 2023 Autumn 2. CCA A300BF , previously a 10-credit course, has been condensed to a 5 credit course with effect from 2020/21 academic year. Students who successfully completed CCA A300BF before the 2020/21 academic year may have their 10 credits counted towards graduation requirements, and will not be required to complete 5 credits of elective course from Table 4. 3. CCA A304BF has been replaced by CCA A306BF with effect from the 2021/22 academic year. If students have successfully completed CCA A304BF, they will be deemed to have satisfied the requirement of CCA A306BF. 4. Course title of CCA A357BF has been updated from “Digital Video Production Workshop: Short Film ” to “Short Film Production” with effect from the 2024 Spring term. 5. Course code of CCA A305BF has been updated to CCA A305CF , and the course title has been updated from “ Digital Video Production Workshop: Television 錄像攝製工作坊: 電視” to “Variety Shows: From TV to Online Media 綜藝節目:從電視到網上媒體” with effect from 2025 Spring term. 6. Course code of CCA A306BF has been updated to CCA A306CF , and the course title has been updated from “ Digital Video Production Workshop: Documentary 錄像攝製工作 坊: 紀錄片” to “ Witness of the Truth: The Craftsmanship on Documentary 看見真相： 紀錄片的製作與探索“with effect from 2024 Autumn term. 7. Course code of CCA A353BF has been updated to CCA A353CF , and the course title has been updated from “ Film, Music and Lyrics 電影、音樂與歌詞” to “Film, Music and Song Lyrics 電影、音樂與歌詞” with effect from 2025 Spring term. 8. Course code of CCA A356BF has been updated to CCA A356CF , and the course title has been updated from “ Masterpieces in Literature 名著選讀 ” to “Studies of Literary Masters 文學大師課” with effect from 2024 Autumn term. 9. Course title of CCA A400BF has been updated from “ Honours Project: Short Screenplay/Fiction Writing/Film Studies/Short Film ” to Honours Project ” with effect from 2024 Autumn term. Honours Classification For the purpose of honours classification of the Bachelor of Arts with Honours in Language Studies and Translation programme, the weighted grade point average (W GPA) will be calculated as follows: (1) Group (a) courses: 40 credits of Higher Level courses from Table 3. (2) Group (b) courses: 40 credits of Middle and Higher Level courses from Tables 1, 2 and [代码: ENGL A107F] [学分: 3]

Students who have completed these courses from the 2023 Autumn Term or thereafter may have the course credits counted to satisfy the requirement of outside discipline courses. 3. Course code of CCA A305BF has been updated to CCA A305CF , and the course title has been updated from “ Digital Video Production Workshop: Television 錄像攝製工作坊:電 視” to “Variety Shows: From TV to Online Media 綜藝節目：從電視到網上媒體” with effect from 2025 Spring term. 4. Course code of CCA A306BF has been updated to CCA A306BF , and the course title has been updated from “Digital Video Production Workshop: Documentary 錄像攝製工作坊: 紀錄片” to Witness of the truth: The Craftsmanship on Documentary 看見真相：紀錄片 的製作與探索” with effect from 2024 Autumn term. 5. Course code of CCA A353BF has been updated to CCA A353CF , and the course title has been updated from “Film, Music and Lyrics 電影、音樂與歌詞” to “Film, Music and Song Lyrics 電影、音樂與歌詞” with effect from 2025 Spring term. Honours Classification For the purpose of honours classification of the Bachelor of Fine Arts with Honours in Animation and Visual Effects programme, the weighted grade point average (WGPA) will be calculated as follows: (1) Group (a) courses consist of the best 40 credits of Higher Level courses from Table 3. (2) Group (b) courses consist of the best 40 credits of Middle and Higher Level course s from Tables 1, 2 and 3, where such credits have not been taken into account for calculation in Group (a) courses. (3) Group (a) and Group (b) courses carry equal weighting when calculating WGPA. II. For students admitted via Year 1 entry before the 2020/21 academic year, Year 2 entry before the 2021/22 academic year, and Year 3 entry before the 2022/23 academic year A student admitted to the programme through Year 1 Entry needs to complete a total of 160 A student is required to complete: 1. 120 credits of core courses in Tables 5, 6, 7 and 8; and 2. 10 credits of outside discipline courses from Table 9; and 3. 10 credits of English Language Enhancement courses *; and * Note: Please refer to the updated list of English Language Enhancement courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_ENGLISH). 4. 20 credits of purpose -designed General Education courses #. # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE). A student admitted to the programme through Year 2 Entry needs to complete a total of 120 required to complete: 1. 100 credits of core courses in Tables 6, 7 and 8; 2. 10 credits of outside discipline courses from Table 9; and 3. 5 credits of English Language Enhancement courses *; and * Note: Please refer to the updated list of English Language Enhancement courses posted on the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_ENGLISH). 4. 5 credits of purpose-designed General Education courses #. # Note: Please refer to the updated list of purpose-designed General Education courses posted in the University website (www.hkmu.edu.hk/FT_GE).
